            }

            to {
                opacity: 1;
                -webkit-transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);
                -moz-transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);
                -ms-transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);
                -o-transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);
                transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);
            }
        }

        @-webkit-keyframes slbEnterPrev {
            from {
                opacity: 0;
                -webkit-transform: translate3d(-4em, 0, 0);
            }

            to {
                opacity: 1;
                -webkit-transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);
            }
        }

        @-moz-keyframes slbEnterPrev {
            from {
                opacity: 0;
                -moz-transform: translate3d(-4em, 0, 0);
            }

            to {
                opacity: 1;
                -moz-transform: translate3d(0, 0, 0);
            }
        }

        @keyframes slbEnterPrev {
            from {
                opacity: 0;
                -webkit-transform: translate3d(-4em, 0, 0);
                -moz-transform: translate3d(-4em, 0, 0);

         $("#iconSearch").click(function () {

             window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
        });
        $("#searchBoxHeader").keypress(function (event) {
            var keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
            if (keycode == '13') {
                window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
            }
        });
        var controller = 'drug';
        controller = controller.toLowerCase();
        var category = '';
        console.log(controller);
        var menuItem = $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item');
        var url = window.location.href.toString().split(window.location.host)[1];
        if (url.includes("image/advancedsearch")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("india/company")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("company")) {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "pillidentifier") {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "drug") {
            if (menuItem[1] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[1]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "company") {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "requestmr") {
           if (menuItem[4] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[4]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else {
            if (menuItem[0] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[0]).addClass('active');
            }
        }

        if (category != null || category != "") {
            if (category == "company") {
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item').removeClass('active');
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item:contains(Find Drug Company)').addClass('active');
            }
        }


        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-xs-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-sm-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-md-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });

    function checkAds(gtag) {
        //MIMSV3-817
        gtag.addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function (event) {
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner', containsAd);
            }
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial', containsAd);
                //if contain Ad,hide verification popup
                if (containsAd) {
                    $('#div-user-profile-modal').hide();
                    $('.jquery-modal').hide();
                }
            }
        });
    }
    function loadDFPadsIn() {
        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-bottom-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-top-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight1');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight2');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight3');

            //$("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-3").parent().show();

           // $("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-5").hide();

        });
    }

            $(document).ready(function () {
            var _mimsclass = "8q";

            if (_mimsclass) {
                var newSubClassCode = [];
                var array = _mimsclass.split(',');

                if (array) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
                        var isNumber = isInt(array[i]);

                        if (isNumber) {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].trim();
                        }
                        else {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].substring(0, array[i].length - 1).trim();
                            isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }

                let uniqueSubClassCode = [...new Set(newSubClassCode)];

                if (uniqueSubClassCode) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < uniqueSubClassCode.length; i++) {
                        HubspotEventTracker(uniqueSubClassCode[i]);
                    }
                    
                }
            }
            
       });

    <script>
     var selectedTab = "BasicPrescribingInfo";
    var selectedMonograph = "BasicPrescribingInfo";
    var vidalMonograph = "VidalPrescribingInfo"

    var x, i, j, selElmnt, a, b, c;
    /* Look for any elements with the class "custom-select": */
    x = document.getElementsByClassName("custom-select");
    for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
        selElmnt = x[i].getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
        /* For each element, create a new DIV that will act as the selected item: */
        if (selectedTab!="") {
        }
        else {
            a = document.createElement("DIV");
            a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
            a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
            a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
            a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[selElmnt.selectedIndex].innerHTML;
            x[i].appendChild(a);
        }


        /* For each element, create a new DIV that will contain the option list: */
        b = document.createElement("DIV");
        b.setAttribute("class", "select-items select-hide");
        for (j = 1; j < selElmnt.length; j++) {
            /* For each option in the original select element,
            create a new DIV that will act as an option item: */
            c = document.createElement("DIV");
            c.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
            c.id = selElmnt.options[j].id;

            if (selectedTab != "") {
                if (selectedMonograph == vidalMonograph && "vidal-" + selectedTab == c.id) {
                        c.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                        a = document.createElement("DIV");
                        a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
                        a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                        a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
                        a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
                        x[i].appendChild(a);
                }
                else {
                    if (selectedTab == c.id) {
                        c.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                        a = document.createElement("DIV");
                        a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
                        a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                        a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
                        a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
                        x[i].appendChild(a);
                    }
                }
            }

            c.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                /* When an item is clicked, update the original select box,
                and the selected item: */
                var y, i, k, s, h;
                s = this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
                h = this.parentNode.previousSibling;
                for (i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
                    if (s.options[i].innerHTML == this.innerHTML) {
                        s.selectedIndex = i;
                        h.innerHTML = this.innerHTML;
                        y = this.parentNode.getElementsByClassName("same-as-selected");
                        for (k = 0; k < y.length; k++) {
                            y[k].removeAttribute("class");
                        }
                        this.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                        var selected = s.options[i].value;
                        //var selectedid = s.options[i].id;
                        //alert("id:" + selectedid);

                        window.location = selected;
                        break;
                    }
                }
                h.click();
            });
            b.appendChild(c);
        }
        x[i].appendChild(b);
        a.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
            /* When the select box is clicked, close any other select boxes,
            and open/close the current select box: */
            e.stopPropagation();
            closeAllSelect(this);
            this.nextSibling.classList.toggle("select-hide");
            if (a.className == "select-selected sel-arrow select-arrow-active") {
                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
            }
            else {

                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");

            }

            this.classList.toggle("select-arrow-active");
        });
    }

    function closeAllSelect(elmnt) {
        /* A function that will close all select boxes in the document,
        except the current select box: */
        var x, y, i, arrNo = [];
        x = document.getElementsByClassName("select-items");
        y = document.getElementsByClassName("select-selected");
        for (i = 0; i < y.length; i++) {
            if (elmnt == y[i]) {
                arrNo.push(i)
            } else {
                y[i].classList.remove("select-arrow-active");
            }
        }
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
            if (arrNo.indexOf(i)) {
                x[i].classList.add("select-hide");
            }
        }
    }
    $(function () {
        var hash = window.location.hash;
        if (hash == "#DrugInteraction") {
            $('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $(hash).offset().top - 80 });
        }
    });
    </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function HubspotEventTracker(subClassCode) {

                var _userEmail = "";

                var _environment = "PRD";
                var _eventName = "";
                var newSubClassCode = "";

                var isNumber = isInt(subClassCode);

                if (isNumber) {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode;
                }
                else {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode.substring(0, subClassCode.length - 1);
                    isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode);
                }

                if (newSubClassCode && isNumber) {
                    if (_environment == "PRD") {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013391463";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013391464";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013391450";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013391453";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                            // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013391239";
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013131929";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013166098";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013131899";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013283175";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                           // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013620143";
                        }
                    }
                }

            if (_eventName) {
                var _hsq = window._hsq = window._hsq || [];
                _hsq.push(
                    ["identify", {
                        email: _userEmail
                    }]);

                _hsq.push(
                    ["trackEvent", {
                        id: _eventName,
                        value: 1
                    }]);
                }

            }

            function isInt(str) {
                return !isNaN(str) && Number.isInteger(parseFloat(str));
            }
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function () {
         $("#iconSearch").click(function () {

             window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
        });
        $("#searchBoxHeader").keypress(function (event) {
            var keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
            if (keycode == '13') {
                window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
            }
        });
        var controller = 'drug';
        controller = controller.toLowerCase();
        var category = '';
        console.log(controller);
        var menuItem = $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item');
        var url = window.location.href.toString().split(window.location.host)[1];
        if (url.includes("image/advancedsearch")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("india/company")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("company")) {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "pillidentifier") {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "drug") {
            if (menuItem[1] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[1]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "company") {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "requestmr") {
           if (menuItem[4] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[4]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else {
            if (menuItem[0] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[0]).addClass('active');
            }
        }

        if (category != null || category != "") {
            if (category == "company") {
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item').removeClass('active');
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item:contains(Find Drug Company)').addClass('active');
            }
        }


        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-xs-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-sm-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-md-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });

        //MIMSV3-1126
        $(document).on('click', '.a_signin', function()
        {
            dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'login',
                'method': 'SSO-Signin'
            });

            //dataLayer.push({'event':'evTracking','evCategory':'URL','evAction':'Click','evLabel':'Sign In','evValue':1})
        })


    });
  </script>

            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("company", company);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("drcsplty", drcSpecialty);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("drc", disease);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("section", section);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("profession", profession);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("specialty", specialty);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("query", searchKeyword);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("sso", sso);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("loggedin", document.getElementById("HiddenLoginStatus").value);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("site_section", "drugs");
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("mobileapp", isMIMSMobileUserAgent);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("occupied_ps_ta_code", occupiedPSTACode);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("occupied_ld_ta_code", occupiedLDTACode);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("occupied_ta_code", occupiedPSTACode);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("priority_ta_code", priorityTACode);
            googletag.enableServices();

            checkAds(googletag.pubads());

        });
        setTimeout('loadDFPadsIn()', 1000);


    }
    else {

        googletag.cmd.push(function () {

            var mappingLeaderboard = googletag.sizeMapping().addSize([1280, 500], [970, 120])
                .addSize([1024, 500], [728, 90]).addSize([768, 500], [728, 90]).addSize([0, 0], [320, 50]).build();

            googletag.defineSlot('/7240521/MIMS_COM_Top_Leaderboard', [970, 120], 'div-gpt-ad-top-leaderboard').defineSizeMapping(mappingLeaderboard).addService(googletag.pubads());
            googletag.defineSlot('/7240521/MIMS_COM_Super_Leaderboard', [970, 120], 'div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard').defineSizeMapping(mappingLeaderboard).addService(googletag.pubads());
            googletag.defineSlot('/7240521/MIMS_COM_PrimeSight', [300, 250], 'div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight1').addService(googletag.pubads());
            googletag.defineSlot('/7240521/MIMS_COM_RIGHT_PRIMESIGHT', [300, 250], 'div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight2').addService(googletag.pubads());
            googletag.defineSlot('/7240521/MIMS_COM_Carousel_PrimeBanner', [300, 100], 'div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight3').addService(googletag.pubads());

            googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
            googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs(true);
            var hdn = document.getElementById("HiddenFieldCountry");
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("com_ctry", hdn.value);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("brand", brand);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("company", company);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("drcsplty", drcSpecialty);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("drc", disease);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("section", section);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("profession", profession);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("specialty", specialty);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("query", searchKeyword);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("sso", sso);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("loggedin", document.getElementById("HiddenLoginStatus").value);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("site_section", "drugs");
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("mobileapp", isMIMSMobileUserAgent);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("occupied_ps_ta_code", occupiedPSTACode);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("occupied_ld_ta_code", occupiedLDTACode);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("occupied_ta_code", occupiedPSTACode);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("priority_ta_code", priorityTACode);
            googletag.enableServices();
            checkAds(googletag.pubads());
        });
        setTimeout('loadDFPAds()', 1000);

    }

    function checkAds(gtag) {
        //MIMSV3-817
        gtag.addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function (event) {
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner', containsAd);
            }
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial', containsAd);
                //if contain Ad,hide verification popup
                if (containsAd) {
                    $('#div-user-profile-modal').hide();
                    $('.jquery-modal').hide();
                }
            }
        });
    }
    function loadDFPadsIn() {
        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-bottom-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-top-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight1');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight2');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight3');

            //$("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-3").parent().show();

           // $("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-5").hide();

        });
    }

    function loadDFPAds() {
        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-top-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight1');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight2');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight3');
            
            
        });
    }

            $(document).ready(function () {
            var _mimsclass = "4i";

            if (_mimsclass) {
                var newSubClassCode = [];
                var array = _mimsclass.split(',');

                if (array) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
                        var isNumber = isInt(array[i]);

                        if (isNumber) {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].trim();
                        }
                        else {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].substring(0, array[i].length - 1).trim();
                            isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }

                let uniqueSubClassCode = [...new Set(newSubClassCode)];

                if (uniqueSubClassCode) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < uniqueSubClassCode.length; i++) {
                        HubspotEventTracker(uniqueSubClassCode[i]);
                    }
                    
                }
            }

            $('.pill-img .prod-img').each(function () {
        var imageid = $(this).attr('id');
        var img = new Image();
        img.onload = function () {
            if (this.width > this.height) {
                $("#" + imageid).attr('style', 'max-width:70%; margin-top:10%');
                $("." + imageid).attr('style', 'max-width:70%; margin-top:10%');
                //$(".thumbs-container-" + imageid.substr(imageid.length - 1) + " img").attr('style', 'max-width:60px;');
            }
            else {
                $("#" + imageid).attr('style', 'max-width:120px; margin-top:0');
                $("." + imageid).attr('style', 'max-width:120px; margin-top:0');
            }
        }
        img.src = $(this).attr('src');

    });

    <script>
     var selectedTab = "ConcisePrescribingInfo";
    var selectedMonograph = "ConcisePrescribingInfo";
    var vidalMonograph = "VidalPrescribingInfo"

    var x, i, j, selElmnt, a, b, c;
    /* Look for any elements with the class "custom-select": */
    x = document.getElementsByClassName("custom-select");
    for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
        selElmnt = x[i].getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
        /* For each element, create a new DIV that will act as the selected item: */
        if (selectedTab!="") {
        }
        else {
            a = document.createElement("DIV");
            a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
            a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
            a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
            a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[selElmnt.selectedIndex].innerHTML;
            x[i].appendChild(a);
        }


        /* For each element, create a new DIV that will contain the option list: */
        b = document.createElement("DIV");
        b.setAttribute("class", "select-items select-hide");
        for (j = 1; j < selElmnt.length; j++) {
            /* For each option in the original select element,
            create a new DIV that will act as an option item: */
            c = document.createElement("DIV");
            c.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
            c.id = selElmnt.options[j].id;

            if (selectedTab != "") {
                if (selectedMonograph == vidalMonograph && "vidal-" + selectedTab == c.id) {
                        c.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                        a = document.createElement("DIV");
                        a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
                        a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                        a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
                        a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
                        x[i].appendChild(a);
                }
                else {
                    if (selectedTab == c.id) {
                        c.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                        a = document.createElement("DIV");
                        a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
                        a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                        a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
                        a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
                        x[i].appendChild(a);
                    }
                }
            }

            c.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                /* When an item is clicked, update the original select box,
                and the selected item: */
                var y, i, k, s, h;
                s = this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
                h = this.parentNode.previousSibling;
                for (i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
                    if (s.options[i].innerHTML == this.innerHTML) {
                        s.selectedIndex = i;
                        h.innerHTML = this.innerHTML;
                        y = this.parentNode.getElementsByClassName("same-as-selected");
                        for (k = 0; k < y.length; k++) {
                            y[k].removeAttribute("class");
                        }
                        this.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                        var selected = s.options[i].value;
                        //var selectedid = s.options[i].id;
                        //alert("id:" + selectedid);

                        window.location = selected;
                        break;
                    }
                }
                h.click();
            });
            b.appendChild(c);
        }
        x[i].appendChild(b);
        a.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
            /* When the select box is clicked, close any other select boxes,
            and open/close the current select box: */
            e.stopPropagation();
            closeAllSelect(this);
            this.nextSibling.classList.toggle("select-hide");
            if (a.className == "select-selected sel-arrow select-arrow-active") {
                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
            }
            else {

                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");

            }

            this.classList.toggle("select-arrow-active");
        });
    }

    function closeAllSelect(elmnt) {
        /* A function that will close all select boxes in the document,
        except the current select box: */
        var x, y, i, arrNo = [];
        x = document.getElementsByClassName("select-items");
        y = document.getElementsByClassName("select-selected");
        for (i = 0; i < y.length; i++) {
            if (elmnt == y[i]) {
                arrNo.push(i)
            } else {
                y[i].classList.remove("select-arrow-active");
            }
        }
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
            if (arrNo.indexOf(i)) {
                x[i].classList.add("select-hide");
            }
        }
    }
    $(function () {
        var hash = window.location.hash;
        if (hash == "#DrugInteraction") {
            $('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $(hash).offset().top - 80 });
        }
    });

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function HubspotEventTracker(subClassCode) {

                var _userEmail = "";

                var _environment = "PRD";
                var _eventName = "";
                var newSubClassCode = "";

                var isNumber = isInt(subClassCode);

                if (isNumber) {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode;
                }
                else {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode.substring(0, subClassCode.length - 1);
                    isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode);
                }

                if (newSubClassCode && isNumber) {
                    if (_environment == "PRD") {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013391463";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013391464";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013391450";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013391453";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                            // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013391239";
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013131929";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013166098";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013131899";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013283175";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                           // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013620143";
                        }
                    }
                }

            if (_eventName) {
                var _hsq = window._hsq = window._hsq || [];
                _hsq.push(
                    ["identify", {
                        email: _userEmail
                    }]);

                _hsq.push(
                    ["trackEvent", {
                        id: _eventName,
                        value: 1
                    }]);
                }

            }

            function isInt(str) {
                return !isNaN(str) && Number.isInteger(parseFloat(str));
            }
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function () {
         $("#iconSearch").click(function () {

             window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
        });
        $("#searchBoxHeader").keypress(function (event) {
            var keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
            if (keycode == '13') {
                window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
            }
        });
        var controller = 'drug';
        controller = controller.toLowerCase();
        var category = '';
        console.log(controller);
        var menuItem = $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item');
        var url = window.location.href.toString().split(window.location.host)[1];
        if (url.includes("image/advancedsearch")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("india/company")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("company")) {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "pillidentifier") {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "drug") {
            if (menuItem[1] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[1]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "company") {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "requestmr") {
           if (menuItem[4] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[4]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else {
            if (menuItem[0] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[0]).addClass('active');
            }
        }

        if (category != null || category != "") {
            if (category == "company") {
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item').removeClass('active');
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item:contains(Find Drug Company)').addClass('active');
            }
        }


        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-xs-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-sm-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-md-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });

        //MIMSV3-1126
        $(document).on('click', '.a_signin', function()
        {
            dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'login',
                'method': 'SSO-Signin'
            });

            //dataLayer.push({'event':'evTracking','evCategory':'URL','evAction':'Click','evLabel':'Sign In','evValue':1})
        })


    });
  </script>

     var hdn = document.getElementById("HiddenFieldCountry");

        null : document.getElementById("HiddenFieldPriorityTACode").value;

    if (hdn.value == "india") {
        googletag.cmd.push(function () {

                .addSize([1024, 500], [728, 90]).addSize([768, 500], [728, 90]).addSize([0, 0], [320, 50]).build();

            googletag.defineSlot('/7240521/CIMS_COM_PrimeSight', [300, 250], 'div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight2').addService(googletag.pubads());

            var hdn = document.getElementById("HiddenFieldCountry");
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("com_ctry", hdn.value);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("brand", brand);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("company", company);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("drcsplty", drcSpecialty);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("drc", disease);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("section", section);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("profession", profession);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("specialty", specialty);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("query", searchKeyword);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("sso", sso);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("loggedin", document.getElementById("HiddenLoginStatus").value);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("site_section", "drugs");

            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("occupied_ld_ta_code", occupiedLDTACode);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("occupied_ta_code", occupiedPSTACode);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("priority_ta_code", priorityTACode);
            googletag.enableServices();

            checkAds(googletag.pubads());

        });
        setTimeout('loadDFPadsIn()', 1000);


    }
    else {

        googletag.cmd.push(function () {

            var mappingLeaderboard = googletag.sizeMapping().addSize([1280, 500], [970, 120])
                .addSize([1024, 500], [728, 90]).addSize([768, 500], [728, 90]).addSize([0, 0], [320, 50]).build();

            googletag.defineSlot('/7240521/MIMS_COM_Top_Leaderboard', [970, 120], 'div-gpt-ad-top-leaderboard').defineSizeMapping(mappingLeaderboard).addService(googletag.pubads());
            googletag.defineSlot('/7240521/MIMS_COM_Super_Leaderboard', [970, 120], 'div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard').defineSizeMapping(mappingLeaderboard).addService(googletag.pubads());
            googletag.defineSlot('/7240521/MIMS_COM_PrimeSight', [300, 250], 'div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight1').addService(googletag.pubads());
            googletag.defineSlot('/7240521/MIMS_COM_RIGHT_PRIMESIGHT', [300, 250], 'div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight2').addService(googletag.pubads());
            googletag.defineSlot('/7240521/MIMS_COM_Carousel_PrimeBanner', [300, 100], 'div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight3').addService(googletag.pubads());

            googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
            googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs(true);
            var hdn = document.getElementById("HiddenFieldCountry");
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("com_ctry", hdn.value);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("brand", brand);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("company", company);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("drcsplty", drcSpecialty);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("drc", disease);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("section", section);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("profession", profession);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("specialty", specialty);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("query", searchKeyword);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("sso", sso);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("loggedin", document.getElementById("HiddenLoginStatus").value);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("site_section", "drugs");
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("mobileapp", isMIMSMobileUserAgent);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("occupied_ps_ta_code", occupiedPSTACode);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("occupied_ld_ta_code", occupiedLDTACode);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("occupied_ta_code", occupiedPSTACode);
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting("priority_ta_code", priorityTACode);
            googletag.enableServices();
            checkAds(googletag.pubads());
        });
        setTimeout('loadDFPAds()', 1000);

    }

    function checkAds(gtag) {
        //MIMSV3-817
        gtag.addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function (event) {
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner', containsAd);
            }
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial', containsAd);
                //if contain Ad,hide verification popup
                if (containsAd) {
                    $('#div-user-profile-modal').hide();
                    $('.jquery-modal').hide();
                }
            }
        });
    }
    function loadDFPadsIn() {
        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-bottom-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-top-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight1');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight2');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight3');

            //$("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-3").parent().show();

           // $("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-5").hide();

        });
    }

    function loadDFPAds() {
        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-top-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight1');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight2');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight3');
            
            
        });
    }
    </script>

         <div class="col-lg-8 monograph-content">
          <div class="monograph-disclaimer-top">
           <a href="#disclaimer">
            This information is not country-specific. Please refer to the Malaysia prescribing information.
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="monograph-header-text">
           Generic Medicine Info
          </div>
          <table>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Indications and Dosage
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               <i>
                Oral
               </i>
               <br/>
               <b>
                Meniere's disease
               </b>
               <br/>
               <div style="padding-left: 20px;">
                <b>
                 Adult:
                </b>
                For the treatment of vertigo, tinnitus, hearing loss, and nausea associated with Meniere's disease: As betahistine dihydrochloride: Initially, 8-16 mg tid. Maintenance: 24-48 mg daily in divided doses. As betahistine mesilate: 6-12 mg tid. Adjust doses according to patient needs.
                <br/>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Administration
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               May be taken with or without food.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Contraindications
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Phaeochromocytoma, active or history of peptic ulcer.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Special Precautions
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Patient with bronchial asthma, CV disease, urticaria, rashes, allergic rhinitis. Patient taking antihistamines. Hepatic impairment. Pregnancy and lactation.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Adverse Reactions
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               <em>
                Significant:
               </em>
               Rarely, ventricular extrasystoles, hypotension, tachycardia.
               <br/>
               <em>
                Gastrointestinal disorders:
               </em>
               Diarrhoea, dry mouth, dyspepsia, nausea. Rarely, mild gastric complaints (e.g. vomiting, gastrointestinal pain, abdominal distension, bloating).
               <br/>
               <em>
                Immune system disorders:
               </em>
               Hypersensitivity reactions (e.g. anaphylaxis).
               <br/>
               <em>
                Nervous system disorders:
               </em>
               Headache.
               <br/>
               <em>
                Skin and subcutaneous tissue disorders:
               </em>
               Rarely, rash, pruritus, urticaria, angioneurotic oedema.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Overdosage
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Symptoms: Nausea, somnolence, abdominal pain; convulsions, pulmonary or cardiac complications. Management: Supportive and symptomatic treatment. Perform gastric lavage.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Drug Interactions
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Metabolism may be inhibited by MAOIs (e.g. selegiline). May diminish efficacy with antihistamines.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Food Interaction
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Delayed absorption with food.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Action
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               <b>
                Description:
               </b>
               <br>
                <b>
                 Mechanism of Action:
                </b>
                Betahistine is a histamine analogue that is claimed to improve the microcirculation of the labyrinth resulting in decreased endolymphatic pressure. The exact mechanism is not yet fully determined; however, it is known to act as both a partial histamine H
                <sub>
                 1
                </sub>
                -receptor agonist and histamine H
                <sub>
                 3
                </sub>
                -receptor antagonist in neuronal tissue, with negligible histamine H
                <sub>
                 2
                </sub>
                -receptor activity. It inhibits presynaptic histamine H
                <sub>
                 3
                </sub>
                -receptors and induces H
                <sub>
                 3
                </sub>
                -receptor downregulation, thus increasing the histamine turnover and release.
                <br>
                 <b>
                  Pharmacokinetics:
                 </b>
                 <br>
                  <b>
                   Absorption:
                  </b>
                  Readily and almost completely absorbed from the gastrointestinal tract. Delayed absorption with food. Time to peak plasma concentration: 1 hour (inactive metabolite).
                  <br>
                   <b>
                    Distribution:
                   </b>
                   Plasma protein binding: &lt;5%.
                   <br/>
                   <b>
                    Metabolism:
                   </b>
                   Rapidly and almost completely metabolised into 2-pyridylacetic acid (inactive metabolite).
                   <br/>
                   <b>
                    Excretion:
                   </b>
                   Via urine (approx 91%; mainly as inactive metabolite). Elimination half-life: Approx 3.5 hours (inactive metabolite).
                   <br/>
                  </br>
                 </br>
                </br>
               </br>
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Chemical Structure
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               <br/>
               <figure>
                <img alt="Chemical Structure Image" src="https://mimsshst.blob.core.windows.net/drug-resources/MY/html/info/Betahistine_01.png"/>
                <figcaption>
                 <strong>
                  Betahistine
                 </strong>
                </figcaption>
                <small>
                 <i>
                  <br/>
                  Source: National Center for Biotechnology Information. PubChem Database. Betahistine, CID=2366, https://pubchem.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/compound/Betahistine (accessed on Jan. 21, 2020)
                 </i>
                </small>
               </figure>
               <br/>
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Storage
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Store between 15-30°C. Protect from moisture and light.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>

                $(document).ready(function () {
            var _mimsclass = "4i";

            if (_mimsclass) {
                var newSubClassCode = [];
                var array = _mimsclass.split(',');

                if (array) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
                        var isNumber = isInt(array[i]);

                        if (isNumber) {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].trim();
                        }
                        else {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].substring(0, array[i].length - 1).trim();
                            isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }

                let uniqueSubClassCode = [...new Set(newSubClassCode)];

                    }
                    
                }

                $("#widget-content1").css("max-height", $("#widget-content1")[0].scrollHeight);

        });

                $("#less4").show();
            } else {
                $("#widget-content4").css("max-height", "370px");
                $("#expand4").show();
                $("#less4").hide();
            }
            $("#widget-content4").toggleClass("truncate");

        });
    });
     </script>

  <script>
   var selectedTab = "ConcisePrescribingInfo";
    var x, i, j, selElmnt, a, b, c;
                                /* Look for any elements with the class "custom-select": */
                                x = document.getElementsByClassName("custom-select");
    for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
        selElmnt = x[i].getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
        /* For each element, create a new DIV that will act as the selected item: */
        if (selectedTab!="") {
        }
        else {
            a = document.createElement("DIV");
            a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
            a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
            a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
            a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[selElmnt.selectedIndex].innerHTML;
            x[i].appendChild(a);
                            }


                            /* For each element, create a new DIV that will contain the option list: */
                            b = document.createElement("DIV");
        b.setAttribute("class", "select-items select-hide");
        for (j = 1; j < selElmnt.length; j++) {
            /* For each option in the original select element,
            create a new DIV that will act as an option item: */
            c = document.createElement("DIV");
            c.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
            c.id = selElmnt.options[j].id;

            if (selectedTab != "") {
                if (selectedTab == c.id) {
                    c.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                    a = document.createElement("DIV");
                    a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
                    a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                    a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
                    a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
                    x[i].appendChild(a);
                        }
            }

            c.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                            /* When an item is clicked, update the original select box,
                            and the selected item: */
                            var y, i, k, s, h;
                            s = this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
                            h = this.parentNode.previousSibling;
                            for (i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
                                if (s.options[i].innerHTML == this.innerHTML) {
                                    s.selectedIndex = i;
                                    h.innerHTML = this.innerHTML;
                                    y = this.parentNode.getElementsByClassName("same-as-selected");
                                    for (k = 0; k < y.length; k++) {
                                        y[k].removeAttribute("class");
                                    }
                                    this.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                                    var selected = s.options[i].value;
                                    //var selectedid = s.options[i].id;
                                    //alert("id:" + selectedid);

                                    window.location = selected;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            h.click();
                        });
            b.appendChild(c);
        }
        x[i].appendChild(b);
                        a.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                            /* When the select box is clicked, close any other select boxes,
                            and open/close the current select box: */
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            closeAllSelect(this);
                            this.nextSibling.classList.toggle("select-hide");
                            if (a.className == "select-selected sel-arrow select-arrow-active") {
                                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
                                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                            }
                            else {

                                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");

                            }

                            this.classList.toggle("select-arrow-active");
                        });
    }

    function closeAllSelect(elmnt) {
                            /* A function that will close all select boxes in the document,
                            except the current select box: */
                            var x, y, i, arrNo = [];
                            x = document.getElementsByClassName("select-items");
                            y = document.getElementsByClassName("select-selected");
                            for (i = 0; i < y.length; i++) {
                                if (elmnt == y[i]) {
                                    arrNo.push(i)
                                } else {
                                    y[i].classList.remove("select-arrow-active");
                                }
                            }
                            for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                                if (arrNo.indexOf(i)) {
                                    x[i].classList.add("select-hide");
                                }
                            }
                        }
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var links = [];


function DropdownSelect(selectedval)
{

              $('.dropdown').on('change', function() {

                var selectedval = $(this).val();
                for (i = 0; i< links.length; i++) {
                            if (links[i] == selectedval.substr(1)) {
                            HideSectionDropdown(selectedval);
                            }
                            else {
                            window.location = selectedval;
                            }
                            }

                            //HideSectionDropdown(selectedval);
                            //window.location = selectedval;
                            });
                            }

                            function HideSectionDropdown(selectedval) {
                            if (selectedval != null) {
                            for (i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
                            if (links[i] != selectedval.substr(1)) {
                            $("#" + links[i]).hide();
                            }
                            }
                            $(selectedval).show();
                            $("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, "slow");
                            }
                            }

                            function HideSection(except_this_id) {
                            $("#inner-section > a").removeClass("drug-group-item-active");
                            $(except_this_id).addClass("drug-group-item-active");

                            for (i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
                            $("#" + links[i]).hide();
                            }

                            $("#" + except_this_id.id.slice(3)).show();
                            $("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, "slow");
                            }
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function HubspotEventTracker(subClassCode) {

                var _userEmail = "";

                var _environment = "PRD";
                var _eventName = "";
                var newSubClassCode = "";

                var isNumber = isInt(subClassCode);

                if (isNumber) {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode;
                }
                else {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode.substring(0, subClassCode.length - 1);
                    isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode);
                }

                if (newSubClassCode && isNumber) {
                    if (_environment == "PRD") {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013391463";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013391464";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013391450";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013391453";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                            // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013391239";
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013131929";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013166098";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013131899";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013283175";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                           // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013620143";
                        }
                    }
                }

            if (_eventName) {
                var _hsq = window._hsq = window._hsq || [];
                _hsq.push(
                    ["identify", {
                        email: _userEmail
                    }]);

                _hsq.push(
                    ["trackEvent", {
                        id: _eventName,
                        value: 1
                    }]);
                }

            }

            function isInt(str) {
                return !isNaN(str) && Number.isInteger(parseFloat(str));
            }
  </script>

   $(document).ready(function () {
         $("#iconSearch").click(function () {

             window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
        });
        $("#searchBoxHeader").keypress(function (event) {
            var keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
            if (keycode == '13') {
                window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
            }
        });
        var controller = 'drug';
        controller = controller.toLowerCase();
        var category = '';
        console.log(controller);
        var menuItem = $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item');
        var url = window.location.href.toString().split(window.location.host)[1];
        if (url.includes("image/advancedsearch")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("india/company")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("company")) {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "pillidentifier") {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "drug") {
            if (menuItem[1] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[1]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "company") {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "requestmr") {
           if (menuItem[4] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[4]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else {
            if (menuItem[0] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[0]).addClass('active');
            }
        }

        if (category != null || category != "") {
            if (category == "company") {
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item').removeClass('active');
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item:contains(Find Drug Company)').addClass('active');
            }
        }


        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-xs-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-sm-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-md-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });

        //MIMSV3-1126
        $(document).on('click', '.a_signin', function()

    function checkAds(gtag) {
        //MIMSV3-817
        gtag.addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function (event) {
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner', containsAd);
            }
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial', containsAd);
                //if contain Ad,hide verification popup
                if (containsAd) {
                    $('#div-user-profile-modal').hide();
                    $('.jquery-modal').hide();
                }
            }
        });
    }
    function loadDFPadsIn() {
        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-bottom-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-top-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight1');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight2');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight3');

            //$("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-3").parent().show();

           // $("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-5").hide();

        });
    }

History of asthma, nasal polyps, angioedema or bronchospasm; GI ulceration or bleeding; haemorrhagic diatheses, operations w/ high risk of haemorrhage or incomplete haemostasis; cerebrovascular bleeding; hypovolaemia, dehydration. Moderate or severe renal impairment. Pregnancy &amp; lactation. Childn &lt;16 yr.

           <script type="text/javascript">
            $(document).ready(function () {
            var _mimsclass = "4l";

            if (_mimsclass) {
                var newSubClassCode = [];
                var array = _mimsclass.split(',');

                if (array) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
                        var isNumber = isInt(array[i]);

                        if (isNumber) {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].trim();
                        }
                        else {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].substring(0, array[i].length - 1).trim();
                            isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }

                let uniqueSubClassCode = [...new Set(newSubClassCode)];

                if (uniqueSubClassCode) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < uniqueSubClassCode.length; i++) {
                        HubspotEventTracker(uniqueSubClassCode[i]);
                    }
                    
                }
            }
            
       });
           </script>

            $('.pill-img .prod-img').each(function () {
        var imageid = $(this).attr('id');
        var img = new Image();
        img.onload = function () {
            if (this.width > this.height) {
                $("#" + imageid).attr('style', 'max-width:70%; margin-top:10%');
                $("." + imageid).attr('style', 'max-width:70%; margin-top:10%');
                //$(".thumbs-container-" + imageid.substr(imageid.length - 1) + " img").attr('style', 'max-width:60px;');
            }
            else {
                $("#" + imageid).attr('style', 'max-width:120px; margin-top:0');
                $("." + imageid).attr('style', 'max-width:120px; margin-top:0');
            }
        }
        img.src = $(this).attr('src');

    });
