    <script>
     var selectedTab = "ConcisePrescribingInfo";
    var selectedMonograph = "ConcisePrescribingInfo";
    var vidalMonograph = "VidalPrescribingInfo"

    var x, i, j, selElmnt, a, b, c;
    /* Look for any elements with the class "custom-select": */
    x = document.getElementsByClassName("custom-select");
    for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
        selElmnt = x[i].getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
        /* For each element, create a new DIV that will act as the selected item: */
        if (selectedTab!="") {
        }
        else {
            a = document.createElement("DIV");
            a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
            a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
            a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
            a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[selElmnt.selectedIndex].innerHTML;
            x[i].appendChild(a);
        }


        /* For each element, create a new DIV that will contain the option list: */
        b = document.createElement("DIV");
        b.setAttribute("class", "select-items select-hide");
        for (j = 1; j < selElmnt.length; j++) {
            /* For each option in the original select element,
            create a new DIV that will act as an option item: */
            c = document.createElement("DIV");
            c.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
            c.id = selElmnt.options[j].id;

            if (selectedTab != "") {
                if (selectedMonograph == vidalMonograph && "vidal-" + selectedTab == c.id) {
                        c.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                        a = document.createElement("DIV");
                        a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
                        a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                        a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
                        a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
                        x[i].appendChild(a);
                }
                else {
                    if (selectedTab == c.id) {
                        c.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                        a = document.createElement("DIV");
                        a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
                        a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                        a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
                        a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
                        x[i].appendChild(a);
                    }
                }
            }

            c.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                /* When an item is clicked, update the original select box,
                and the selected item: */
                var y, i, k, s, h;
                s = this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
                h = this.parentNode.previousSibling;
                for (i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
                    if (s.options[i].innerHTML == this.innerHTML) {
                        s.selectedIndex = i;
                        h.innerHTML = this.innerHTML;
                        y = this.parentNode.getElementsByClassName("same-as-selected");
                        for (k = 0; k < y.length; k++) {
                            y[k].removeAttribute("class");
                        }
                        this.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                        var selected = s.options[i].value;
                        //var selectedid = s.options[i].id;
                        //alert("id:" + selectedid);

                        window.location = selected;
                        break;
                    }
                }
                h.click();
            });
            b.appendChild(c);
        }
        x[i].appendChild(b);
        a.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
            /* When the select box is clicked, close any other select boxes,
            and open/close the current select box: */
            e.stopPropagation();
            closeAllSelect(this);
            this.nextSibling.classList.toggle("select-hide");
            if (a.className == "select-selected sel-arrow select-arrow-active") {
                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
            }
            else {

                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");

            }

            this.classList.toggle("select-arrow-active");
        });
    }

    function closeAllSelect(elmnt) {
        /* A function that will close all select boxes in the document,
        except the current select box: */
        var x, y, i, arrNo = [];
        x = document.getElementsByClassName("select-items");
        y = document.getElementsByClassName("select-selected");
        for (i = 0; i < y.length; i++) {
            if (elmnt == y[i]) {
                arrNo.push(i)
            } else {
                y[i].classList.remove("select-arrow-active");
            }
        }
        for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
            if (arrNo.indexOf(i)) {
                x[i].classList.add("select-hide");
            }
        }
    }
    $(function () {
        var hash = window.location.hash;
        if (hash == "#DrugInteraction") {
            $('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: $(hash).offset().top - 80 });
        }
    });
    </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function HubspotEventTracker(subClassCode) {

                var _userEmail = "";

                var _environment = "PRD";
                var _eventName = "";
                var newSubClassCode = "";

                var isNumber = isInt(subClassCode);

                if (isNumber) {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode;
                }
                else {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode.substring(0, subClassCode.length - 1);
                    isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode);
                }

                if (newSubClassCode && isNumber) {
                    if (_environment == "PRD") {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013391463";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013391464";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013391450";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013391453";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                            // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013391239";
                        }
                    }
                    else {

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function () {
         $("#iconSearch").click(function () {

             window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
        });
        $("#searchBoxHeader").keypress(function (event) {
            var keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
            if (keycode == '13') {
                window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
            }
        });
        var controller = 'drug';
        controller = controller.toLowerCase();
        var category = '';
        console.log(controller);
        var menuItem = $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item');
        var url = window.location.href.toString().split(window.location.host)[1];
        if (url.includes("image/advancedsearch")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("india/company")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("company")) {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "pillidentifier") {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "drug") {
            if (menuItem[1] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[1]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "company") {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "requestmr") {
           if (menuItem[4] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[4]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else {
            if (menuItem[0] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[0]).addClass('active');
            }
        }

        if (category != null || category != "") {
            if (category == "company") {
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item').removeClass('active');
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item:contains(Find Drug Company)').addClass('active');
            }
        }


        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-xs-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-sm-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-md-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });

        //MIMSV3-1126
        $(document).on('click', '.a_signin', function()
        {
            dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'login',
                'method': 'SSO-Signin'
            });

            //dataLayer.push({'event':'evTracking','evCategory':'URL','evAction':'Click','evLabel':'Sign In','evValue':1})
        })


    });
  </script>

    function checkAds(gtag) {
        //MIMSV3-817
        gtag.addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function (event) {
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner', containsAd);
            }
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial', containsAd);
                //if contain Ad,hide verification popup
                if (containsAd) {
                    $('#div-user-profile-modal').hide();
                    $('.jquery-modal').hide();
                }
            }
        });
    }
    function loadDFPadsIn() {
        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-bottom-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-top-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight1');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight2');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight3');

            //$("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-3").parent().show();

           // $("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-5").hide();

        });
    }

    function loadDFPAds() {

            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight1');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight2');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight3');
            
            
        });
    }

               <div style="padding-left: 20px;">
                <b>
                 Adult:
                </b>
                As 0.1, 0.15 or 0.2% soln: Instill 1 drop into affected eye(s) bid or tid (approx 8 or 12 hrly).

               </div>

               </i>

               <b>
                Rosacea
               </b>
               <br/>
               <div style="padding-left: 20px;">
                <b>
                 Adult:
                </b>
                As 0.33% gel: Apply pea-sized amount once daily as a thin layer across the entire face covering each of the 5 areas of the face (forehead, nose, chin and each cheek).

               </div>

Ocular hyperaemia, burning/ stinging sensation, blurred vision, ocular allergic reaction, conjunctival follicles, corneal staining/erosion, photophobia, eyelid erythema, ocular dryness, ocular pain, conjunctival blanching, conjunctival discharge, iritis, iridocyclitis, miosis, fatigue, drowsiness, dizziness, asthenia, abnormal taste, blepharitis, depression, nasal dryness, palpitation, arrhythmias, hypotension, syncope,  headache, blurred vision, dry mouth, eyelid oedema (ophth).

             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Patient Counseling Information
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               This drug may cause fatigue and/or drowsiness, if affected, do not drive or operate machinery. Avoid exposure to excessive sunlight and UV irradiation (topical). Remove contact lenses prior to ophth admin and reinsert after 15 min.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Monitoring Parameters
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Monitor IOP routinely.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Drug Interactions
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               TCAs (e.g. imipramine) and tetracyclic antidepressants (e.g. mianserin) that affect the metabolism and uptake of circulating amines may interfere w/ IOP-lowering effect brimonidine. Additive IOP-lowering and CV effects w/ β-blockers, antihypertensives, cardiac glycosides. Additive or potentiating effect w/ CNS depressants (e.g. barbiturates, opiates, sedatives or anaesthetics).
               <br/>
               <strong>
                Potentially Fatal:
               </strong>
               Interfered metabolism and increased adverse effect when used w/ MAOIs (e.g. selegiline).
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Food Interaction
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Additive CNS depressant effect w/ alcohol.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Action
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               <b>
                Description:
               </b>
               <br>
                <b>
                 Mechanism of Action:
                </b>
                Brimonidine is an α
                <sub>
                 2
                </sub>
                -adrenoceptor agonist. As an ophthalmic agent, it works to reduce aqueous humour production and increase uveoscleral flow, thus lowering intraocular pressure (IOP). Topically, it reduces erythema through direct cutaneous vasoconstriction.
                <br/>
                <b>
                 Onset:
                </b>
                Rapid (ophth).
                <br/>
                <b>
                 Duration:
                </b>
                ≥12 hr (ophth).
                <br/>
                <b>
                 Pharmacokinetics:
                </b>
                <br/>
                <b>
                 Absorption:
                </b>
                Time to peak plasma concentration: Approx 0.5-4 hr (ophth); approx after 15 days (topical).
                <br/>
                <b>
                 Metabolism:
                </b>
                Extensive hepatic metabolism.
                <br/>
                <b>
                 Excretion:
                </b>
                Via urine. Elimination half-life: Approx 2-3 hr (ophth).
                <br/>
               </br>
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Chemical Structure
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               <br/>
               <figure>
                <img alt="Chemical Structure Image" src="https://mimsshst.blob.core.windows.net/drug-resources/MY/html/info/Brimonidine_01.png"/>
                <figcaption>
                 <strong>
                  Brimonidine
                 </strong>
                </figcaption>
                <small>
                 <i>
                  <br/>
                  Source: National Center for Biotechnology Information. PubChem Compound Summary for CID 2435, Brimonidine. https://pubchem.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/compound/Brimonidine. Accessed Nov. 28, 2022.
                 </i>
                </small>
               </figure>
               <br/>
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Storage
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Store between 15-25°C.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>

               <script type="text/javascript">
                $(document).ready(function () {
            var _mimsclass = "14f";

            if (_mimsclass) {
                var newSubClassCode = [];
                var array = _mimsclass.split(',');

                if (array) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
                        var isNumber = isInt(array[i]);

                        if (isNumber) {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].trim();
                        }
                        else {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].substring(0, array[i].length - 1).trim();
                            isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }

                let uniqueSubClassCode = [...new Set(newSubClassCode)];

                if (uniqueSubClassCode) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < uniqueSubClassCode.length; i++) {
                        HubspotEventTracker(uniqueSubClassCode[i]);
                    }
                    
                }
            }

  <script>
   var selectedTab = "ConcisePrescribingInfo";
    var x, i, j, selElmnt, a, b, c;
                                /* Look for any elements with the class "custom-select": */
                                x = document.getElementsByClassName("custom-select");
    for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
        selElmnt = x[i].getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
        /* For each element, create a new DIV that will act as the selected item: */
        if (selectedTab!="") {
        }
        else {
            a = document.createElement("DIV");
            a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
            a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
            a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
            a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[selElmnt.selectedIndex].innerHTML;
            x[i].appendChild(a);
                            }


                            /* For each element, create a new DIV that will contain the option list: */
                            b = document.createElement("DIV");
        b.setAttribute("class", "select-items select-hide");
        for (j = 1; j < selElmnt.length; j++) {
            /* For each option in the original select element,
            create a new DIV that will act as an option item: */
            c = document.createElement("DIV");
            c.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
            c.id = selElmnt.options[j].id;

            if (selectedTab != "") {
                if (selectedTab == c.id) {
                    c.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                    a = document.createElement("DIV");
                    a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
                    a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                    a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
                    a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
                    x[i].appendChild(a);
                        }
            }

            c.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                            /* When an item is clicked, update the original select box,
                            and the selected item: */
                            var y, i, k, s, h;
                            s = this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
                            h = this.parentNode.previousSibling;
                            for (i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
                                if (s.options[i].innerHTML == this.innerHTML) {
                                    s.selectedIndex = i;
                                    h.innerHTML = this.innerHTML;
                                    y = this.parentNode.getElementsByClassName("same-as-selected");
                                    for (k = 0; k < y.length; k++) {
                                        y[k].removeAttribute("class");
                                    }
                                    this.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                                    var selected = s.options[i].value;
                                    //var selectedid = s.options[i].id;
                                    //alert("id:" + selectedid);

                                    window.location = selected;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            h.click();
                        });
            b.appendChild(c);
        }
        x[i].appendChild(b);
                        a.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                            /* When the select box is clicked, close any other select boxes,
                            and open/close the current select box: */
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            closeAllSelect(this);
                            this.nextSibling.classList.toggle("select-hide");
                            if (a.className == "select-selected sel-arrow select-arrow-active") {
                                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
                                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                            }
                            else {

                                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");

                            }

                            this.classList.toggle("select-arrow-active");
                        });
    }

    function closeAllSelect(elmnt) {
                            /* A function that will close all select boxes in the document,
                            except the current select box: */
                            var x, y, i, arrNo = [];
                            x = document.getElementsByClassName("select-items");
                            y = document.getElementsByClassName("select-selected");
                            for (i = 0; i < y.length; i++) {
                                if (elmnt == y[i]) {
                                    arrNo.push(i)
                                } else {
                                    y[i].classList.remove("select-arrow-active");
                                }
                            }
                            for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                                if (arrNo.indexOf(i)) {
                                    x[i].classList.add("select-hide");
                                }
                            }
                        }
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var links = [];


function DropdownSelect(selectedval)
{

              $('.dropdown').on('change', function() {

                var selectedval = $(this).val();
                for (i = 0; i< links.length; i++) {
                            if (links[i] == selectedval.substr(1)) {
                            HideSectionDropdown(selectedval);
                            }
                            else {
                            window.location = selectedval;
                            }
                            }

                            //HideSectionDropdown(selectedval);
                            //window.location = selectedval;
                            });
                            }

                            function HideSectionDropdown(selectedval) {
                            if (selectedval != null) {
                            for (i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
                            if (links[i] != selectedval.substr(1)) {
                            $("#" + links[i]).hide();
                            }
                            }
                            $(selectedval).show();
                            $("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, "slow");
                            }
                            }

                            function HideSection(except_this_id) {
                            $("#inner-section > a").removeClass("drug-group-item-active");
                            $(except_this_id).addClass("drug-group-item-active");

                            for (i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
                            $("#" + links[i]).hide();
                            }

                            $("#" + except_this_id.id.slice(3)).show();
                            $("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, "slow");
                            }
  </script>

   function HubspotEventTracker(subClassCode) {

                var _userEmail = "";

                var _environment = "PRD";
                var _eventName = "";
                var newSubClassCode = "";

                var isNumber = isInt(subClassCode);

                if (isNumber) {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode;
                }
                else {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode.substring(0, subClassCode.length - 1);
                    isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode);
                }

                if (newSubClassCode && isNumber) {
                    if (_environment == "PRD") {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013391463";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013391464";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013391450";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013391453";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                            // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013391239";
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013131929";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013166098";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013131899";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013283175";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                           // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013620143";
                        }
                    }
                }

            if (_eventName) {
                var _hsq = window._hsq = window._hsq || [];
                _hsq.push(
                    ["identify", {
                        email: _userEmail
                    }]);

                _hsq.push(
                    ["trackEvent", {
                        id: _eventName,
                        value: 1
                    }]);
                }

            }

            function isInt(str) {
                return !isNaN(str) && Number.isInteger(parseFloat(str));
            }
  </script>

            element = document.getElementById("signInLink");
            if (element && document.body.contains(element)) {
                element.click();
            }
        }

    });

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function () {
         $("#iconSearch").click(function () {

             window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
        });
        $("#searchBoxHeader").keypress(function (event) {
            var keycode = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
            if (keycode == '13') {
                window.location.href = 'https://www.mims.com/malaysia/drug/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent($("#searchBoxHeader").val()) +'&mtype=brand';
            }
        });
        var controller = 'drug';
        controller = controller.toLowerCase();
        var category = '';
        console.log(controller);
        var menuItem = $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item');
        var url = window.location.href.toString().split(window.location.host)[1];
        if (url.includes("image/advancedsearch")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("india/company")) {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (url.includes("company")) {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "pillidentifier") {
            if (menuItem[2] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[2]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "drug") {
            if (menuItem[1] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[1]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "company") {
            if (menuItem[3] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[3]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else if (controller == "requestmr") {
           if (menuItem[4] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[4]).addClass('active');
            }
        }
        else {
            if (menuItem[0] != undefined) {
                $(menuItem[0]).addClass('active');
            }
        }

        if (category != null || category != "") {
            if (category == "company") {
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item').removeClass('active');
                $('#subMenu').find('.main-menu .item:contains(Find Drug Company)').addClass('active');
            }
        }


        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBar").removeClass("sticker-bar");
                $("#stickyBar").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 50) {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("hidden-lg-up");
            } else {
                $("#stickyBarMobile").removeClass("sticker-bar-mobile");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-xs-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-sm-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("show-md-down");
                $("#stickyBarMobile").addClass("hidden-lg-up");
            }
        });

        //MIMSV3-1126
        $(document).on('click', '.a_signin', function()
        {
            dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'login',
                'method': 'SSO-Signin'
            });

            //dataLayer.push({'event':'evTracking','evCategory':'URL','evAction':'Click','evLabel':'Sign In','evValue':1})
        })


    });

    function checkAds(gtag) {
        //MIMSV3-817
        gtag.addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function (event) {
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner', containsAd);
            }
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial', containsAd);
                //if contain Ad,hide verification popup
                if (containsAd) {
                    $('#div-user-profile-modal').hide();
                    $('.jquery-modal').hide();
                }
            }
        });
    }
    function loadDFPadsIn() {
        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-bottom-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-top-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight1');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight2');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight3');

            //$("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-3").parent().show();

           // $("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-5").hide();

        });
    }

    function loadDFPAds() {

            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight1');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight2');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-mims-primesight3');
            
            
        });
    }

             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Indications and Dosage
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               <i>
                Oral
               </i>
               <br/>
               <b>
                Echinococcosis
               </b>
               <br/>
               <div style="padding-left: 20px;">
                <b>
                 Adult:
                </b>
                As treatment of cystic hydatid disease of the liver, lung and peritoneum: &lt;60 kg: 15 mg/kg daily in 2 divided doses, up to Max total daily dose of 800 mg; ≥60 kg: 400 mg bid. Doses are given for 28 days followed by a 14-day drug-free period for a total of 3 cycles. Treatment and dosing recommendations may vary among individual products and between countries (refer to specific product guidelines).
                <br/>
               </div>
               <br/>
               <i>
                Oral
               </i>
               <br/>
               <b>
                Neurocysticercosis
               </b>
               <br/>
               <div style="padding-left: 20px;">
                <b>
                 Adult:
                </b>
                As treatment of parenchymal neurocysticercosis: &lt;60 kg: 15 mg/kg daily in 2 divided doses, up to Max total daily dose of 800 mg; ≥60 kg: 400 mg bid. Doses are given for 8-30 days. Initiate concomitant appropriate corticosteroid or anticonvulsant therapy as needed. Treatment and dosing recommendations may vary among individual products and between countries (refer to specific product guidelines).
                <br/>
               </div>
               <br/>
               <i>
                Oral
               </i>
               <br/>
               <b>
                Ascariasis, Enterobiasis, Hookworm infections, Trichuriasis
               </b>
               <br/>
               <div style="padding-left: 20px;">
                <b>
                 Adult:
                </b>
                400 mg as a single dose. Treatment and dosing recommendations may vary among individual products and between countries (refer to specific product guidelines).
                <br/>
                <b>
                 Child:
                </b>
                <em>
                 1-2 years
                </em>
                200 mg as a single dose;
                <em>
                 &gt;2 years
                </em>

           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Administration
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Should be taken with food. For systemic infections, administer w/ high-fat meal to increase absorption. For patients w/ swallowing difficulty, tab may be crushed/chewed.
               <br/>
               Should be taken on an empty stomach. For intraluminal infections w/o systemic involvement, take on an empty stomach. For patients w/ swallowing difficulty, tab may be crushed/chewed.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Contraindications
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Hypersensitivity. Pregnancy.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Special Precautions
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Patient with cysticercosis retinal lesions. May worsen symptoms of neurocysticercosis by inducing an inflammatory response. Hepatic impairment. Children. Lactation.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Adverse Reactions
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               <em>
                Significant:
               </em>
               Bone marrow suppression, aplastic anaemia, agranulocytosis; mild to moderate elevation of liver enzymes, hepatitis, acute liver failure.
               <br/>
               <em>
                Blood and lymphatic system disorders:
               </em>
               Leucopenia, neutropenia.
               <br/>
               <em>
                Gastrointestinal disorders:
               </em>
               Nausea, vomiting, abdominal pain, diarrhoea.
               <br/>
               <em>
                General disorders and administration site conditions:
               </em>
               Fever.
               <br/>
               <em>
                Nervous system disorders:
               </em>
               Dizziness, headache.
               <br/>
               <em>
                Skin and subcutaneous tissue disorders:
               </em>
               Alopecia.
               <br/>
               <strong>
                Potentially Fatal:
               </strong>
               Granulocytopenia or pancytopenia.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               <a href="/pregdef" title="Categorization of risk of drug use in pregnancy from the United States Food &amp; Drug Administration">
                Pregnancy Category (US FDA)
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               PO: C
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Monitoring Parameters
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Evaluate pregnancy status in women of childbearing potential before therapy. Perform ophthalmic exams for the presence of retinal lesions before treatment initiation when used for neurocysticercosis. Monitor liver enzymes (transaminases) before the start of each treatment cycle and at least every 2 weeks during therapy. Monitor CBC with differential. Assess for signs and symptoms of cerebral hypertension, focal neurologic deficits or seizures.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Drug Interactions
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Concurrent use with cimetidine, dexamethasone and praziquantel increases the plasma concentrations of albendazole sulfoxide (active metabolite). Concomitant use with carbamazepine, phenobarbital and phenytoin significantly decreases the concentration of albendazole sulfoxide.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Food Interaction
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Increased bioavailability with fatty meals or grapefruit juice.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Action
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               <b>
                Description:
               </b>
               <br>
                <b>
                 Mechanism of Action:
                </b>
                Albendazole, a benzimidazole derivative, binds to free β-tubulin in parasite cells. This results in selective inhibition of parasite microtubule polymerisation and inhibition of microtubule-dependent glucose uptake. Insufficient glucose causes a lack of adenosine triphosphate (ATP) resulting in the death of the parasite.
                <br>
                 <b>
                  Pharmacokinetics:
                 </b>
                 <br>
                  <b>
                   Absorption:
                  </b>
                  Poorly absorbed from the gastrointestinal tract. Increased bioavailability with a fatty meal. Time to peak plasma concentration: 2-5 hours (albendazole sulfoxide).
                  <br>
                   <b>
                    Distribution:
                   </b>
                   Widely distributed throughout the body including bile, cyst fluid or wall, CSF, liver and urine. Enters breast milk. Plasma protein binding: 70%.
                   <br>
                    <b>
                     Metabolism:
                    </b>
                    Metabolised in the liver via rapid sulfoxidation into albendazole sulfoxide (active metabolite), then further metabolised into albendazole sulfone and other primary oxidative metabolites. Undergoes extensive first-pass metabolism.
                    <br>
                     <b>
                      Excretion:
                     </b>
                     Via urine (&lt;1% as active metabolite); faeces. Elimination half-life: 8-12 hours (albendazole sulfoxide).
                     <br>
                     </br>
                    </br>
                   </br>
                  </br>
                 </br>
                </br>
               </br>
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Chemical Structure
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               <br/>

                 </i>
                </small>
               </figure>
               <br/>
              </div>

            </td>

              </div>

              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>

  <script>
   var selectedTab = "ConcisePrescribingInfo";
    var x, i, j, selElmnt, a, b, c;
                                /* Look for any elements with the class "custom-select": */
                                x = document.getElementsByClassName("custom-select");
    for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
        selElmnt = x[i].getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
        /* For each element, create a new DIV that will act as the selected item: */
        if (selectedTab!="") {
        }
        else {
            a = document.createElement("DIV");
            a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
            a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
            a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
            a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[selElmnt.selectedIndex].innerHTML;
            x[i].appendChild(a);
                            }


                            /* For each element, create a new DIV that will contain the option list: */
                            b = document.createElement("DIV");
        b.setAttribute("class", "select-items select-hide");
        for (j = 1; j < selElmnt.length; j++) {
            /* For each option in the original select element,
            create a new DIV that will act as an option item: */
            c = document.createElement("DIV");
            c.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
            c.id = selElmnt.options[j].id;

            if (selectedTab != "") {
                if (selectedTab == c.id) {
                    c.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                    a = document.createElement("DIV");
                    a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
                    a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                    a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
                    a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
                    x[i].appendChild(a);
                        }
            }

            c.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                            /* When an item is clicked, update the original select box,
                            and the selected item: */
                            var y, i, k, s, h;
                            s = this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
                            h = this.parentNode.previousSibling;
                            for (i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
                                if (s.options[i].innerHTML == this.innerHTML) {
                                    s.selectedIndex = i;
                                    h.innerHTML = this.innerHTML;
                                    y = this.parentNode.getElementsByClassName("same-as-selected");
                                    for (k = 0; k < y.length; k++) {
                                        y[k].removeAttribute("class");
                                    }
                                    this.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                                    var selected = s.options[i].value;
                                    //var selectedid = s.options[i].id;
                                    //alert("id:" + selectedid);

                                    window.location = selected;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            h.click();
                        });
            b.appendChild(c);
        }
        x[i].appendChild(b);
                        a.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                            /* When the select box is clicked, close any other select boxes,
                            and open/close the current select box: */
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            closeAllSelect(this);
                            this.nextSibling.classList.toggle("select-hide");
                            if (a.className == "select-selected sel-arrow select-arrow-active") {
                                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
                                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                            }
                            else {

                                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");

                            }

                            this.classList.toggle("select-arrow-active");
                        });
    }

    function closeAllSelect(elmnt) {
                            /* A function that will close all select boxes in the document,
                            except the current select box: */
                            var x, y, i, arrNo = [];
                            x = document.getElementsByClassName("select-items");
                            y = document.getElementsByClassName("select-selected");
                            for (i = 0; i < y.length; i++) {
                                if (elmnt == y[i]) {
                                    arrNo.push(i)
                                } else {
                                    y[i].classList.remove("select-arrow-active");
                                }
                            }
                            for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                                if (arrNo.indexOf(i)) {
                                    x[i].classList.add("select-hide");
                                }
                            }
                        }
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var links = [];


function DropdownSelect(selectedval)
{

              $('.dropdown').on('change', function() {

                var selectedval = $(this).val();
                for (i = 0; i< links.length; i++) {
                            if (links[i] == selectedval.substr(1)) {
                            HideSectionDropdown(selectedval);
                            }
                            else {
                            window.location = selectedval;
                            }
                            }

                            //HideSectionDropdown(selectedval);
                            //window.location = selectedval;
                            });
                            }

                            function HideSectionDropdown(selectedval) {
                            if (selectedval != null) {
                            for (i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
                            if (links[i] != selectedval.substr(1)) {
                            $("#" + links[i]).hide();
                            }
                            }
                            $(selectedval).show();
                            $("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, "slow");
                            }
                            }

                            function HideSection(except_this_id) {
                            $("#inner-section > a").removeClass("drug-group-item-active");
                            $(except_this_id).addClass("drug-group-item-active");

                            for (i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
                            $("#" + links[i]).hide();
                            }

                            $("#" + except_this_id.id.slice(3)).show();
                            $("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, "slow");
                            }
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function HubspotEventTracker(subClassCode) {

                var _userEmail = "";

                var _environment = "PRD";
                var _eventName = "";
                var newSubClassCode = "";

                var isNumber = isInt(subClassCode);

                if (isNumber) {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode;
                }
                else {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode.substring(0, subClassCode.length - 1);
                    isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode);
                }

                if (newSubClassCode && isNumber) {
                    if (_environment == "PRD") {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013391463";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013391464";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013391450";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013391453";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                            // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013391239";
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013131929";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013166098";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013131899";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013283175";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                           // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013620143";
                        }
                    }
                }

            if (_eventName) {
                var _hsq = window._hsq = window._hsq || [];
                _hsq.push(
                    ["identify", {
                        email: _userEmail
                    }]);

                _hsq.push(
                    ["trackEvent", {
                        id: _eventName,
                        value: 1
                    }]);
                }

            }

            function isInt(str) {
                return !isNaN(str) && Number.isInteger(parseFloat(str));
            }
  </script>

    function checkAds(gtag) {
        //MIMSV3-817
        gtag.addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function (event) {
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-announcement-banner', containsAd);
            }
            if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() == "div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial") {
                var containsAd = !event.isEmpty;
                console.log('div-gpt-ad-mims-com-front-interstitial', containsAd);
                //if contain Ad,hide verification popup
                if (containsAd) {
                    $('#div-user-profile-modal').hide();
                    $('.jquery-modal').hide();
                }
            }
        });
    }
    function loadDFPadsIn() {
        googletag.cmd.push(function () {
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-bottom-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-top-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-super-leaderboard');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight1');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight2');
            googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-cims-primesight3');

            //$("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-3").parent().show();

           // $("#div-gpt-ad-1389534547398-5").hide();

        });
    }

               </i>
               <br/>
               <b>
                Replacement of fluid and electrolytes
               </b>

                <b>
                 Adult:
                </b>

                <br/>
                <b>
                 Child:
                </b>
                0.9% used as nasal drops.
                <br/>
               </div>
               <br/>
               <i>
                Oral
               </i>
               <br/>

                 Adult:
                </b>

               <i>
                Oral
               </i>
               <br/>
               <b>
                Chronic salt-losing conditions
               </b>

           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Contraindications
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Conditions whereby admin of sodium chloride would be detrimental. Not to be used to induce emesis. Sustained release tablets: GI disorders associated with strictures or diverticula.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Special Precautions
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Hypertension, heart failure, peripheral or pulmonary oedema, impaired renal function, liver cirrhosis, preeclampsia. Maintain adequate water intake. Pregnancy.  Inj of 3 or 5% sodium chloride solution should be given via a large vein at a rate not exceeding 100 ml/hr. Monitor fluid balance, serum electrolytes and acid base balance espcially during prolonged treatment. Caution when used in patients who are receiving corticosteroids or corticotropin.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Adverse Reactions
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               Hypernatraemia; thirst, reduced salivation and lachrymation, fever, tachycardia, hypertension, headache, dizziness, restlessness, irritability and weakness.
               <br/>
               <strong>
                Potentially Fatal:
               </strong>
               Intra-amniotic inj of hypertonic solutions: Disseminated intravascular coagulation, renal necrosis, cervical and uterine lesions, pulmonary embolism, pneumonia and death.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">

               <a href="/pregdef" title="Categorization of risk of drug use in pregnancy from the United States Food &amp; Drug Administration">

               </a>

              </div>
             </div>
            </td>

              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Drug Interactions
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               May affect serum concentrations of lithium.
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>

           <tr>
            <td>
             <div id="">
              <div class="monograph-section-header">
               Action
              </div>
              <div class="monograph-section-content">
               <b>
                Description:
               </b>
               <br>
                <b>
                 Mechanism of Action:
                </b>
                Sodium chloride is the major extracellular cation. It is important in electrolyte and fluid balance, osmotic pressure control and water distribution as it restores sodium ions. It is used as a source of electrolytes and water for hydration, treatment of metabolic acidosis, priming solution in haemodialysis and treatment of hyperosmolar diabetes. It is also used as diluents for infusion of compatible drug additives.
                <br>
                 <b>
                  Pharmacokinetics:
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <b>
                  Absorption:
                 </b>
                 Well-absorbed from the GI tract.
                 <br/>
                 <b>
                  Excretion:
                 </b>
                 Mainly in the urine, with small amounts excreted in the sweat, faeces, tears and saliva.
                 <br/>
                </br>
               </br>
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>

               <script type="text/javascript">
                $(document).ready(function () {
            var _mimsclass = "13d, 19, 3d, 14i, 15e";

            if (_mimsclass) {
                var newSubClassCode = [];
                var array = _mimsclass.split(',');

                if (array) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
                        var isNumber = isInt(array[i]);

                        if (isNumber) {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].trim();
                        }
                        else {
                            newSubClassCode[i] = array[i].substring(0, array[i].length - 1).trim();
                            isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }

                let uniqueSubClassCode = [...new Set(newSubClassCode)];

                if (uniqueSubClassCode) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < uniqueSubClassCode.length; i++) {
                        HubspotEventTracker(uniqueSubClassCode[i]);
                    }
                    
                }
            }
            
       });
               </script>
              </div>
             </div>
            </td>
           </tr>
          </table>

     <script>
      var selectedTab = "ConcisePrescribingInfo";
    var x, i, j, selElmnt, a, b, c;
                                /* Look for any elements with the class "custom-select": */
                                x = document.getElementsByClassName("custom-select");
    for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
        selElmnt = x[i].getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
        /* For each element, create a new DIV that will act as the selected item: */
        if (selectedTab!="") {
        }
        else {
            a = document.createElement("DIV");
            a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
            a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
            a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
            a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[selElmnt.selectedIndex].innerHTML;
            x[i].appendChild(a);
                            }


                            /* For each element, create a new DIV that will contain the option list: */
                            b = document.createElement("DIV");
        b.setAttribute("class", "select-items select-hide");
        for (j = 1; j < selElmnt.length; j++) {
            /* For each option in the original select element,
            create a new DIV that will act as an option item: */
            c = document.createElement("DIV");
            c.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
            c.id = selElmnt.options[j].id;

            if (selectedTab != "") {
                if (selectedTab == c.id) {
                    c.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                    a = document.createElement("DIV");
                    a.setAttribute("class", "select-selected sel-arrow");
                    a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                    a.setAttribute("id", "cs");
                    a.innerHTML = selElmnt.options[j].innerHTML;
                    x[i].appendChild(a);
                        }
            }

            c.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                            /* When an item is clicked, update the original select box,
                            and the selected item: */
                            var y, i, k, s, h;
                            s = this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName("select")[0];
                            h = this.parentNode.previousSibling;
                            for (i = 0; i < s.length; i++) {
                                if (s.options[i].innerHTML == this.innerHTML) {
                                    s.selectedIndex = i;
                                    h.innerHTML = this.innerHTML;
                                    y = this.parentNode.getElementsByClassName("same-as-selected");
                                    for (k = 0; k < y.length; k++) {
                                        y[k].removeAttribute("class");
                                    }
                                    this.setAttribute("class", "same-as-selected");
                                    var selected = s.options[i].value;
                                    //var selectedid = s.options[i].id;
                                    //alert("id:" + selectedid);

                                    window.location = selected;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                            h.click();
                        });
            b.appendChild(c);
        }
        x[i].appendChild(b);
                        a.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                            /* When the select box is clicked, close any other select boxes,
                            and open/close the current select box: */
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            closeAllSelect(this);
                            this.nextSibling.classList.toggle("select-hide");
                            if (a.className == "select-selected sel-arrow select-arrow-active") {
                                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");
                                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                            }
                            else {

                                a.removeAttribute("aria-expanded", "false");
                                a.setAttribute("aria-expanded", "true");

                            }

                            this.classList.toggle("select-arrow-active");
                        });
    }

    function closeAllSelect(elmnt) {
                            /* A function that will close all select boxes in the document,
                            except the current select box: */
                            var x, y, i, arrNo = [];
                            x = document.getElementsByClassName("select-items");
                            y = document.getElementsByClassName("select-selected");
                            for (i = 0; i < y.length; i++) {
                                if (elmnt == y[i]) {
                                    arrNo.push(i)
                                } else {
                                    y[i].classList.remove("select-arrow-active");
                                }
                            }
                            for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
                                if (arrNo.indexOf(i)) {
                                    x[i].classList.add("select-hide");
                                }
                            }
                        }
     </script>
     <script type="text/javascript">
      var links = [];


function DropdownSelect(selectedval)
{

              $('.dropdown').on('change', function() {

                var selectedval = $(this).val();
                for (i = 0; i< links.length; i++) {
                            if (links[i] == selectedval.substr(1)) {
                            HideSectionDropdown(selectedval);
                            }
                            else {
                            window.location = selectedval;
                            }
                            }

                            //HideSectionDropdown(selectedval);
                            //window.location = selectedval;
                            });
                            }

                            function HideSectionDropdown(selectedval) {
                            if (selectedval != null) {
                            for (i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
                            if (links[i] != selectedval.substr(1)) {
                            $("#" + links[i]).hide();
                            }
                            }
                            $(selectedval).show();
                            $("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, "slow");
                            }
                            }

                            function HideSection(except_this_id) {
                            $("#inner-section > a").removeClass("drug-group-item-active");
                            $(except_this_id).addClass("drug-group-item-active");

                            for (i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
                            $("#" + links[i]).hide();
                            }

                            $("#" + except_this_id.id.slice(3)).show();
                            $("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, "slow");
                            }
     </script>

   function HubspotEventTracker(subClassCode) {

                var _userEmail = "";

                var _environment = "PRD";
                var _eventName = "";
                var newSubClassCode = "";

                var isNumber = isInt(subClassCode);

                if (isNumber) {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode;
                }
                else {
                    newSubClassCode = subClassCode.substring(0, subClassCode.length - 1);
                    isNumber = isInt(newSubClassCode);
                }

                if (newSubClassCode && isNumber) {
                    if (_environment == "PRD") {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013391463";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013391464";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013391450";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013391453";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                            // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013391239";
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        if (newSubClassCode == "1" || newSubClassCode == "11") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Alimentary Tract & Metabolic";
                            _eventName = "000013131929";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "2") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Cardiovascular System";
                            _eventName = "000013166098";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "8") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - General Anti-Infectives Systemic";
                            _eventName = "000013131899";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "4") {
                            //_eventName = "PV for TA - Nervous System";
                            _eventName = "000013283175";
                        }
                        else if (newSubClassCode == "3") {
                           // _eventName = "PV for TA - Respiratory System";
                            _eventName = "000013620143";
                        }
                    }
                }

            if (_eventName) {
                var _hsq = window._hsq = window._hsq || [];
                _hsq.push(
                    ["identify", {
                        email: _userEmail
                    }]);

                _hsq.push(
                    ["trackEvent", {
                        id: _eventName,
                        value: 1
                    }]);
                }

            }

            function isInt(str) {
                return !isNaN(str) && Number.isInteger(parseFloat(str));
            }

    var secondSpan = document.getElementById("interval");
    var urlHref = document.getElementById("url");
    var url = urlHref.getAttribute("href");
    var second = 5;
    setInterval(function () {
        second--;
        if (second >= 0) {
            secondSpan.innerHTML = second;
        }
        if (second == 0) {
            window.location = url;
        }
    }, 1000);
